THROUGH THE INFORMATION LISTED ON THE MEETING AGENDA. INDIVIDUALS IN THE 
COUNCIL CHAMBER MAY SIGN UP TO TESTIFY WITH A STAFF MEMBER LOCATED AT THE 
DESK IN THE 8TH FLOOR LOBBY. INDIVIDUALS AT COURTESY TESTIMONY SITES MAY 
SIGN UP WITH STAFF AT THE SITE, AND INDIVIDUALS PARTICIPATING REMOTELY 
MAY SIGN UP IN THE MEETING CHAT. INDIVIDUALS CONNECTED BY PHONE ARE ON 
MUTE AND SHOULD UNMUTE WHEN THEY WISH TO TESTIFY.\r\n\r\nINDIVIDUALS 
SHOULD KEEP THEIR VIDEOS AND MICROPHONES OFF AND TURN IT ON ONLY WHEN 
IT'S THEIR TIME TO TESTIFY. TESTIMONY IS LIMITED TO THE ITEMS LISTED ON 
THE AGENDA AND INDIVIDUALS MAY TESTIFY UP TO THREE MINUTES WITH ONE 
MINUTE TO CONCLUDE PER ITEM. WHEN TESTIFYING, PLEASE STATE YOUR NAME AND 
THE NAME OF ANY ORGANIZATION YOU REPRESENT, AS WELL AS THE ITEMS ON WHICH 
YOU WILL BE TESTIFYING. PLEASE ALSO IDENTIFY TO THE COUNCIL IF YOU ARE A 
PAID LOBBYIST. INDIVIDUALS MAY ALSO BE DISCONNECTED FROM THE MEETING AT

RESOLUTION NO. 22-265 EXPRESSING APPRECIATION TO MAYOR MICHAEL P. 
VICTORINO WHEREAS, MAYOR MICHAEL P. VICTORINO LUCK LEAVING OFFICE ON 
JANUARY 2ND, 2023, HAVING SERVED AS MAYOR OF MAUI COUNTY SINCE 2019 AND 
AS A COUNCIL MEMBER FOR CONSECUTIVE TERMS FROM 2007 TO 2017; AND WHEREAS, 
MAYOR VICTORINO WAS BORN TO WILLIAM AND IRENE VICTORINO, RAISED IN HILO, 
HAWAI'I AND GRADUATED FROM HILO HIGH SCHOOL IN 1970; AND WHEREAS, MAYOR 
VICTORINO HAS BEEN MARRIED TO HIS WIFE JOYCELYN VICTORINO FOR OVER 49 
YEARS, TWO SONS MICHAEL, JR. AND SHANE, FIVE GRAND CHILDREN KELCIE, 
AARON, KEENAN, KALIA, KINGSTON AND THREE GREAT- GRANDCHILDREN AMAIYAH, 
AKAMU AND TIVOLI; AND WHEREAS, MAYOR VICTORINO ATTENDED HILO COLLEGE, 
HAWAI'I COMMUNITY COLLEGE AND MAUI COMMUNITY COLLEGE, MAJORING IN 
BUSINESS ADMINISTRATION AND MINORING IN LAW AND HOTEL MANAGEMENT; AND 
WHEREAS, MAYOR VICTORINO HAS SERVED ON THE BOARDS OF NONPROFITS COMMUNITY 
AND GOVERNMENT ORGANIZATIONS, INCLUDING AMERICAN WATER WORKS ASSOCIATION, 
HAWAI'I CONFERENCE OF MAYORS, HAWAI'I STATE BOARD OF EDUCATION, JAPANESE 
CULTURAL SOCIETY OF MAUI, MAUI COUNTY BOARD OF WATER SUPPLY MAUI ECONOMIC 
CONCERNS OF THE COMMUNITY MAUI ECONOMIC DEVELOPMENT BOARD, MAUI FAMILY 
SERVICES MAUI JAYCEES AND HAWAI'I STATE JAYCEES, WAIHE'E COMMUNITY 
ASSOCIATION, WAIPU COMMUNITY ASSOCIATION AND WAILUKU COMMUNITY THE 
ASSOCIATION; AND WHEREAS, DURING HIS TENURE AS MAUI COUNTY'S CHIEF 
EXECUTIVE, MAYOR VICTORINO PROVIDED STEADY LEADERSHIP DURING 
UNPRECEDENTED NATURAL DISASTERS, INCLUDING WILDFIRES, DROUGHT AND 
FLOODING; AND WHEREAS, MAYOR VICTORINO LED MAUI COUNTY'S RESPONSE TO THE 
COVID-19 PANDEMIC, THE WORST PUBLIC HEALTH AND ECONOMIC CRISIS OF RECENT 
HISTORY, MAINTAINING ESSENTIAL COUNTY SERVICES WHILE WORK SIDE-BY-SIDE 
WITH THE GOVERNOR, AND STATE HAWAI'I HEALTH OFFICIALS TO PROTECTION THE 
HEALTH AND WELL-BEING OF MAUI COUNTY RESIDENTS AND WHEREAS, MAYOR 
VICTORINO ESTABLISHED THE OFFICE OF CLIMATE CHANGE, RESILIENCY, AND 
SUSTAINABILITY TO PROTECT COMMUNITY WELL-BEING DURING A TIME OF CHANGING 
CLIMATE AND MORE FREQUENT SEVERE WEATHER; AND WHEREAS, MAYOR VICTORINO'S 
PLANS FOR THE COUNTY'S HALAU OF 'OIWI ART THE WORLD'S FIRST PURPOSE 
DESIGNED HOME FOR THE STUDY, PRACTICE AND PERFORMANCE OF HULA AND 
ASSOCIATED ARTS; AND WHEREAS, MAYOR VICTORINO ACQUIRED 45 ACRES OF 
SIGNIFICANT COASTAL LANDS AT NO COST TO MAUI COUNTY TAXPAYERS TO 
ESTABLISH THE NORTH SHORE PRESERVATION ZONE; AND WHEREAS, MAYOR VICTORINO 
SECURED A PUBLIC-PRIVATE PARTNERSHIP AGREEMENT WITH WAIKAPU COUNTRY TOWN 
PROJECT PROVIDING 213 ADDITIONAL RESIDENTIAL WORKFORCE HOUSING UNITS, 
INCLUDING INFRASTRUCTURE CONTRIBUTIONS CONSISTING OF NEW CIRCLE MAUI 
WASTEWATER RECLAMATION FACILITY AND THE EXTENSION OF WAIALAE ROAD; AND 
WHEREAS, MAYOR VICTORINO EXPEDITED DEVELOPMENT OF AFFORDABLE AND 
OBTAINABLE HOUSING FOR RESIDENTS INCLUDING MORE THAN 1200 NEW UNITS 
DURING HIS TERM, WITH NEARLY 750 UNDER CONSTRUCTION AND 4622 APPROVED FOR 
CONSTRUCTION; AND WHERE'S MAYOR VICTORINO'S DEDICATION TO PUBLIC SERVICE

WHEN AND FOR ALWAYS BEING TO -- I LIKE THE WORD "TENACIOUS," BECAUSE I 
THINK SHE IS TENACIOUS ABOUT FOLLOWING UP ON THINGS THAT ARE DEAR AND 
PASSIONATE TO HER HEART. YOUR HUMAN CONCERNS AND PARK COMMITTEE MET 
NOVEMBER 28, 2022 TO DISCUSS RESOLUTION 22-252 ENTITLED "URGING THE STATE 
LEGISLATURE AND GOVERNOR OF THE STATE OF HAWAI'I TO PROVIDE FOR THE 
ESTABLISHMENT OF THE PROPOSED WEST MAUI HOSPITAL AND MEDICAL CENTER." 
RESOLUTION 22-252, ITS PURPOSE IS TO URGE THE HAWAI'I STATE LEGISLATURE 
AND THE GOVERNOR TO PROVIDER FUNDING FOR THE PROVIDERS OF WEST MAUI 
HOSPITAL AND MEDICAL CENTER. YOUR COMMITTEE NOTES THE ONLY ACUTE CARE 
HOSPITAL IN MAUI ISLAND IS MAUI MEMORIAL MEDICAL CENTER, WHICH DUE TO 
LIMITED INFRASTRUCTURE, IMPACT FROM CLIMATE CHANGE AND NATURAL DISASTERS, 
AND TRAFFIC, CAN BE A CHALLENGE TO ACCESS FROM THE WEST SIDE, ESPECIALLY 
DURING TIMES OF EMERGENCIES.\r\n\r\nYOUR COMMITTEE NOTES THAT 
UNPRECEDENTED GROWTH IN VISITORS AND RESIDENTS WILL USUALLY INCREASE 
HEALTH CARE DEMANDS FOR AN UNDER UNDERSERVED WEST MAUI POPULATION. WEST 
MAUI HOSPITAL AND MEDICAL CENTER WILL PROVIDE AN ACUTE CARE HOSPITAL ON 
THE WEST SIDE, WITH VITAL 24-HOUR EMERGENCY SERVICES AND PHARMACEUTICAL 
ACCESS TO RESIDENTS AND VISITORS. YOUR COMMITTEE FURTHER NOTED NEWPORT 
HOSPITAL CORPORATION A CALIFORNIA-BASED DEVELOPER HAS OBTAINED THE 
REQUIRED OFF-INFRASTRUCTURE, WATER AND SEWER TIMES AND CRITICAL 
CERTIFICATE OF NEED FOR THE PROPOSED FIDELITY NEWPORT HOSPITAL 
CORPORATION WILL PROVIDE A LONG-TERM LAND LEASE TO THE HOSPITAL 
FOUNDATION TO BUILD ON AND OPERATE THE HOSPITAL. THE COUNCIL'S ADOPTION 
OF RESOLUTION 22-252 WILL SHOW GOVERNMENTAL SUPPORT NEEDED TO SEEK $7 
MILLION IN GRANT-IN-AID FUNDING FROM THE STATE TO PAY FOR NECESSARY 
INFRASTRUCTURE, WHICH IF SECURED, WILL LEVERAGE FEDERAL FUNDING. YOUR 
COMMITTEE NOTED THIS IS A TIME-SENSITIVE MATTER, AS THE DEADLINE TO APPLY 
FOR GRANT-IN-AID FUNDING IS DECEMBER 2022. YOUR COMMITTEE VOTED:45 0 TO 
RECOMMEND ADOPTION OF RESOLUTION 22-3525, CD 1. I RESPECTFULLY ASK FOR 
THE MEMBERS SUPPORT OF MY MOTION. THANK YOU. >> ANY MORE

THANK YOU, CHAIR, THE BILL'S PURPOSE TO AMEND THE COMPREHENSIVE ORDINANCE 
TO CLARIFY TEMPORAL USE FALLS WITHIN THE DEFINITION OF TIME SHARE PLAN TO 
AMELIORATE LODGING CHALLENGES THAT HEALTH CARE PROVIDERS FACE BY
